NewCtxClient to configure client\n   111→type Option func(*Client)\n   112→\n   113→// NewFromURL creates a new etcdv3 client from a URL.\n   114→func NewFromURL(url string) (*Client, error) {\n   115→\treturn New(Config{Endpoints: []string{url}})\n   116→}\n   117→\n   118→// NewFromURLs creates a new etcdv3 client from URLs.\n   119→func NewFromURLs(urls []string) (*Client, error) {\n   120→\treturn New(Config{Endpoints: urls})\n   121→}\n   122→\n   123→// WithZapLogger is a NewCtxClient option that overrides the logger\n   124→func WithZapLogger(lg *zap.Logger) Option {\n   125→\treturn func(c *Client) {\n   126→\t\tc.lg.Store(lg)\n   127→\t}\n   128→}\n   129→\n   130→// WithLogger overrides the logger.\n   131→//\n   132→// Deprecated: Please use WithZapLogger or Logger field in clientv3.Config\n   133→//\n   134→// Does not changes grpcLogger, that can be explicitly configured\n   135→// using grpc_zap.ReplaceGrpcLoggerV2(..) method.\n   136→func (c *Client) WithLogger(lg *zap.Logger) *Client {\n   137→\tc.lg.Store(lg)\n   138→\treturn c\n   139→}\n   140→\n   141→// GetLogger gets the logger.\n   142→// NOTE: This method is for internal use of etcd-client library and should not be used as general-purpose logger.\n   143→func (c *Client) GetLogger() *zap.Logger {\n   144→\treturn c.lg.Load()\n   145→}\n   146→\n   147→// Close shuts down the client's etcd connections.\n   148→func (c *Client) Close() error {\n   149→\tc.cancel()\n   150→\tif c.Watcher != nil {\n   151→\t\tc.Watcher.Close()\n   152→\t}\n   153→\tif c.Lease != nil {\n   154→\t\tc.Lease.Close()\n   155→\t}\n   156→\tif c.conn != nil {\n   157→\t\treturn ContextError(c.ctx, c.conn.Close())\n   158→\t}\n   159→\treturn c.ctx.Err()\n   160→}\n   161→\n   162→// Ctx is a context for \"out of band\" messages (e.g., for sending\n   163→// \"clean up\" message when another context is canceled). It is\n   164→// canceled on client Close().\n   165→func (c *Client) Ctx() context.Context { return c.ctx }\n   166→\n   167→// Endpoints lists the registered endpoints for the client.\n   168→func (c *Client) Endpoints() []string {\n   169→\t// copy the slice; protect original endpoints from being changed\n   170→\tc.epMu.RLock()\n   171→\tdefer c.epMu.RUnlock()\n   172→\teps := make([]string, len(c.endpoints))\n   173→\tcopy(eps, c.endpoints)\n   174→\treturn eps\n   175→}\n   176→\n   177→// SetEndpoints updates client's endpoints.\n   178→func (c *Client) SetEndpoints(eps ...string) {\n   179→\tc.epMu.Lock()\n   180→\tdefer c.epMu.Unlock()\n   181→\tc.endpoints = eps\n   182→\n   183→\tc.resolver.SetEndpoints(eps)\n   184→}\n   185→\n   186→// Sync synchronizes client's endpoints with the known endpoints from the etcd membership.\n   187→func (c *Client) Sync(ctx context.Context) error {\n   188→\tmresp, err := c.MemberList(ctx)\n   189→\tif err != nil {\n   190→\t\treturn err\n   191→\t}\n   192→\tvar eps []string\n   193→\tfor _, m := range mresp.Members {\n   194→\t\tif len(m.Name) != 0 && !m.IsLearner {\n   195→\t\t\teps = append(eps, m.ClientURLs...)\n   196→\t\t}\n   197→\t}\n   198→\t// The linearizable `MemberList` returned successfully, so the\n   199→\t// endpoints shouldn't be empty.\n   200→\tverify.Verify(\"empty endpoints returned from etcd cluster\", func() (bool, map[string]any) {\n   201→\t\treturn len(eps) > 0, nil\n   202→\t})\n   203→\tc.SetEndpoints(eps...)\n   204→\tc.GetLogger().Debug(\"set etcd endpoints by autoSync\", zap.Strings(\"endpoints\", eps))\n   205→\treturn nil\n   206→}\n   207→\n   208→func (c *Client) autoSync() {\n   209→\tif c.cfg.AutoSyncInterval == time.Duration(0) {\n   210→\t\treturn\n   211→\t}\n   212→\n   213→\tfor {\n   214→\t\tselect {\n   215→\t\tcase <-c.ctx.Done():\n   216→\t\t\treturn\n   217→\t\tcase <-time.After(c.cfg.AutoSyncInterval):\n   218→\t\t\tctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(c.ctx, 5*time.Second)\n   219→\t\t\terr := c.Sync(ctx)\n   220→\t\t\tcancel()\n   221→\t\t\tif err != nil && !errors.Is(err, c.ctx.Err()) {\n   222→\t\t\t\tc.GetLogger().Info(\"Auto sync endpoints failed.\", zap.Error(err))\n   223→\t\t\t}\n   224→\t\t}\n   225→\t}\n   226→}\n   227→\n   228→// dialSetupOpts gives the dial opts prior to any authentication.\n   229→func (c *Client) dialSetupOpts(creds grpccredentials.TransportCredentials, dopts ...grpc.DialOption) []grpc.DialOption {\n   230→\tvar opts []grpc.DialOption\n   231→\n   232→\tif c.cfg.DialKeepAliveTime > 0 {\n   233→\t\tparams := keepalive.ClientParameters{\n   234→\t\t\tTime:                c.cfg.DialKeepAliveTime,\n   235→\t\t\tTimeout:             c.cfg.DialKeepAliveTimeout,\n   236→\t\t\tPermitWithoutStream: c.cfg.PermitWithoutStream,\n   237→\t\t}\n   238→\t\topts = append(opts, grpc.WithKeepaliveParams(params))\n   239→\t}\n   240→\topts = append(opts, dopts...)\n   241→\n   242→\tif creds != nil {\n   243→\t\topts = append(opts, grpc.WithTransportCredentials(creds))\n   244→\t} else {\n   245→\t\topts = append(opts, grpc.WithTransportCredentials(insecure.NewCredentials()))\n   246→\t}\n   247→\n   248→\tunaryMaxRetries := defaultUnaryMaxRetries\n   249→\tif c.cfg.MaxUnaryRetries > 0 {\n   250→\t\tunaryMaxRetries = c.cfg.MaxUnaryRetries\n   251→\t}\n   252→\n   253→\tbackoffWaitBetween := defaultBackoffWaitBetween\n   254→\tif c.cfg.BackoffWaitBetween > 0 {\n   255→\t\tbackoffWaitBetween = c.cfg.BackoffWaitBetween\n   256→\t}\n   257→\n   258→\tbackoffJitterFraction := defaultBackoffJitterFraction\n   259→\tif c.cfg.BackoffJitterFraction > 0 {\n   260→\t\tbackoffJitterFraction = c.cfg.BackoffJitterFraction\n   261→\t}\n   262→\n   263→\t// Interceptor retry and backoff.\n   264→\t// TODO: Replace all of clientv3/retry.go with RetryPolicy:\n   265→\t// https://github.com/grpc/grpc-proto/blob/cdd9ed5c3d3f87aef62f373b93361cf7bddc620d/grpc/service_config/service_config.proto#L130\n   266→\trrBackoff := withBackoff(c.roundRobinQuorumBackoff(backoffWaitBetween, backoffJitterFraction))\n   267→\topts = append(opts,\n   268→\t\t// Disable stream retry by default since go-grpc-middleware/retry does not support client streams.\n   269→\t\t// Streams that are safe to retry are enabled individually.\n   270→\t\tgrpc.WithStreamInterceptor(c.streamClientInterceptor(withMax(0), rrBackoff)),\n   271→\t\tgrpc.WithUnaryInterceptor(c.unaryClientInterceptor(withMax(unaryMaxRetries), rrBackoff)),\n   272→\t)\n   273→\n   274→\treturn opts\n   275→}\n   276→\n   277→// Dial connects to a single endpoint using the client's config.\n   278→func (c *Client) Dial(ep string) (*grpc.ClientConn, error) {\n   279→\tcreds := c.credentialsForEndpoint(ep)\n   280→\n   281→\t// Using ad-hoc created resolver, to guarantee only explicitly given\n   282→\t// endpoint is used.\n   283→\treturn c.dial(creds, grpc.WithResolvers(resolver.New(ep)))\n   284→}\n   285→\n   286→func (c *Client) getToken(ctx context.Context) error {\n   287→\tvar err error // return last error in a case of fail\n   288→\n   289→\tif c.Token != \"\" {\n   290→\t\tc.authTokenBundle.UpdateAuthToken(c.Token)\n   291→\t\treturn nil\n   292→\t}\n   293→\n   294→\tif c.Username == \"\" || c.Password == \"\" {\n   295→\t\treturn nil\n   296→\t}\n   297→\n   298→\tresp, err := c.Auth.Authenticate(ctx, c.Username, c.Password)\n   299→\tif err != nil {\n   300→\t\tif errors.Is(err, rpctypes.ErrAuthNotEnabled) {\n   301→\t\t\tc.authTokenBundle.UpdateAuthToken(\"\")\n   302→\t\t\treturn nil\n   303→\t\t}\n   304→\t\treturn err\n   305→\t}\n   306→\tc.authTokenBundle.UpdateAuthToken(resp.Token)\n   307→\treturn nil\n   308→}\n   309→\n   310→// dialWithBalancer dials the client's current load balanced resolver group.  The scheme of the host\n   311→// of the provided endpoint determines the scheme used for all endpoints of the client connection.\n   312→func (c *Client) dialWithBalancer(dopts ...grpc.DialOption) (*grpc.ClientConn, error) {\n   313→\tcreds := c.credentialsForEndpoint(c.Endpoints()[0])\n   314→\topts := append(dopts, grpc.WithResolvers(c.resolver))\n   315→\treturn c.dial(creds, opts...)\n   316→}\n   317→\n   318→// dial configures and dials any grpc balancer target.\n   319→func (c *Client) dial(creds grpccredentials.TransportCredentials, dopts ...grpc.DialOption) (*grpc.ClientConn, error) {\n   320→\topts := c.dialSetupOpts(creds, dopts...)\n   321→\n   322→\tif c.authTokenBundle != nil {\n   323→\t\topts = append(opts, grpc.WithPerRPCCredentials(c.authTokenBundle.PerRPCCredentials()))\n   324→\t}\n   325→\n   326→\topts = append(opts, c.cfg.DialOptions...)\n   327→\n   328→\ttarget := fmt.Sprintf(\"%s://%p/%s\", resolver.Schema, c, authority(c.endpoints[0]))\n   329→\tconn, err := grpc.NewClient(target, opts...)\n   330→\tif err != nil {\n   331→\t\treturn nil, err\n   332→\t}\n   333→\tif dialTimeout := c.cfg.DialTimeout; dialTimeout > 0 {\n   334→\t\tdctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(c.ctx, dialTimeout)\n   335→\t\tdefer cancel()\n   336→\n   337→\t\tif err := waitForConnection(dctx, conn); err != nil {\n   338→\t\t\tconn.Close()\n   339→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   340→\t\t}\n   341→\t}\n   342→\treturn conn, nil\n   343→}\n   344→\n   345→func waitForConnection(ctx context.Context, conn *grpc.ClientConn) error {\n   346→\tcli := healthpb.NewHealthClient(conn)\n   347→\n   348→\t// Use WaitForReady to wait until the connection is ready. The health check\n   349→\t// may return Unimplemented if the server does not expose the health endpoint,\n   350→\t// or FailedPrecondition if the leader has not yet applied the configuration\n   351→\t// change that enables it. In both cases, we can still treat the connection as\n   352→\t// healthy enough to proceed.\n   353→\t//\n   354→\t// Use withMax to disable retrying on Unimplemented, so that we can\n   355→\t// return the original error immediately.\n   356→\t_, err := cli.Check(ctx, &healthpb.HealthCheckRequest{}, grpc.WaitForReady(true), withMax(0))\n   357→\tif err == nil {\n   358→\t\treturn nil\n   359→\t}\n   360→\tif cerr := ctx.Err(); cerr != nil {\n   361→\t\tif serr, ok := status.FromError(err); ok && serr.Message() != \"\" {\n   362→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"etcdclient: failed to connect to the etcd server: %s: %w\", serr.Message(), cerr)\n   363→\t\t}\n   364→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"etcdclient: failed to connect to the etcd server: %w\", cerr)\n   365→\t}\n   366→\n   367→\tserr, ok := status.FromError(err)\n   368→\tif ok {\n   369→\t\tswitch serr.Code() {\n   370→\t\tcase codes.Unimplemented, codes.FailedPrecondition:\n   371→\t\t\treturn nil\n   372→\t\t}\n   373→\t}\n   374→\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"etcdclient: failed to dial by invoking health endpoint: %w\", err)\n   375→}\n   376→\n   377→func authority(endpoint string) string {\n   378→\tspl := strings.SplitN(endpoint, \"://\", 2)\n   379→\tif len(spl) < 2 {\n   380→\t\tif strings.HasPrefix(endpoint, \"unix:\") {\n   381→\t\t\treturn endpoint[len(\"unix:\"):]\n   382→\t\t}\n   383→\t\tif strings.HasPrefix(endpoint, \"unixs:\") {\n   384→\t\t\treturn endpoint[len(\"unixs:\"):]\n   385→\t\t}\n   386→\t\treturn endpoint\n   387→\t}\n   388→\treturn spl[1]\n   389→}\n   390→\n   391→func (c *Client) credentialsForEndpoint(ep string) grpccredentials.TransportCredentials {\n   392→\tr := endpoint.RequiresCredentials(ep)\n   393→\tswitch r {\n   394→\tcase endpoint.CredsDrop:\n   395→\t\treturn nil\n   396→\tcase endpoint.CredsOptional:\n   397→\t\treturn c.creds\n   398→\tcase endpoint.CredsRequire:\n   399→\t\tif c.creds != nil {\n   400→\t\t\treturn c.creds\n   401→\t\t}\n   402→\t\treturn credentials.NewTransportCredential(nil)\n   403→\tdefault:\n   404→\t\tpanic(fmt.Errorf(\"unsupported CredsRequirement: %v\", r))\n   405→\t}\n   406→}\n   407→\n   408→func newClient(cfg *Config) (*Client, error) {\n   409→\tif cfg == nil {\n   410→\t\tcfg = &Config{}\n   411→\t}\n   412→\tvar creds grpccredentials.TransportCredentials\n   413→\tif cfg.TLS != nil {\n   414→\t\tcreds = credentials.NewTransportCredential(cfg.TLS)\n   415→\t}\n   416→\n   417→\tif cfg.Token != \"\" && (cfg.Username != \"\" || cfg.Password != \"\") {\n   418→\t\treturn nil, ErrMutuallyExclusiveCfg\n   419→\t}\n   420→\n   421→\t// use a temporary skeleton client to bootstrap first connection\n   422→\tbaseCtx := context.TODO()\n   423→\tif cfg.Context != nil {\n   424→\t\tbaseCtx = cfg.Context\n   425→\t}\n   426→\n   427→\tctx, cancel := context.WithCancel(baseCtx)\n   428→\tclient := &Client{\n   429→\t\tconn:     nil,\n   430→\t\tcfg:      *cfg,\n   431→\t\tcreds:    creds,\n   432→\t\tctx:      ctx,\n   433→\t\tcancel:   cancel,\n   434→\t\tepMu:     new(sync.RWMutex),\n   435→\t\tcallOpts: defaultCallOpts,\n   436→\t}\n   437→\n   438→\tvar err error\n   439→\tvar lg *zap.Logger\n   440→\tif cfg.Logger != nil {\n   441→\t\tlg = cfg.Logger\n   442→\t} else if cfg.LogConfig != nil {\n   443→\t\tlg, err = cfg.LogConfig.Build()\n   444→\t} else {\n   445→\t\tlg, err = logutil.CreateDefaultZapLogger(ClientLogLevel())\n   446→\t\tif lg != nil {\n   447→\t\t\tlg = lg.Named(\"etcd-client\")\n   448→\t\t}\n   449→\t}\n   450→\tif err != nil {\n   451→\t\treturn nil, err\n   452→\t}\n   453→\tclient.lg.Store(lg)\n   454→\n   455→\tif cfg.Username != \"\" && cfg.Password != \"\" {\n   456→\t\tclient.Username = cfg.Username\n   457→\t\tclient.Password = cfg.Password\n   458→\t\tclient.authTokenBundle = credentials.NewPerRPCCredentialBundle()\n   459→\t}\n   460→\n   461→\tif cfg.Token != \"\" {\n   462→\t\tclient.Token = cfg.Token\n   463→\t\tclient.authTokenBundle = credentials.NewPerRPCCredentialBundle()\n   464→\t}\n   465→\n   466→\tif cfg.MaxCallSendMsgSize > 0 || cfg.MaxCallRecvMsgSize > 0 {\n   467→\t\tif cfg.MaxCallRecvMsgSize > 0 && cfg.MaxCallSendMsgSize > cfg.MaxCallRecvMsgSize {\n   468→\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"gRPC message recv limit (%d bytes) must be greater than send limit (%d bytes)\", cfg.MaxCallRecvMsgSize, cfg.MaxCallSendMsgSize)\n   469→\t\t}\n   470→\t\tcallOpts := []grpc.CallOption{\n   471→\t\t\tdefaultWaitForReady,\n   472→\t\t\tdefaultMaxCallSendMsgSize,\n   473→\t\t\tdefaultMaxCallRecvMsgSize,\n   474→\t\t}\n   475→\t\tif cfg.MaxCallSendMsgSize > 0 {\n   476→\t\t\tcallOpts[1] = grpc.MaxCallSendMsgSize(cfg.MaxCallSendMsgSize)\n   477→\t\t}\n   478→\t\tif cfg.MaxCallRecvMsgSize > 0 {\n   479→\t\t\tcallOpts[2] = grpc.MaxCallRecvMsgSize(cfg.MaxCallRecvMsgSize)\n   480→\t\t}\n   481→\t\tclient.callOpts = callOpts\n   482→\t}\n   483→\n   484→\tclient.resolver = resolver.New(cfg.Endpoints...)\n   485→\n   486→\tif len(cfg.Endpoints) < 1 {\n   487→\t\tclient.cancel()\n   488→\t\treturn nil, errors.New(\"at least one Endpoint is required in client config\")\n   489→\t}\n   490→\tclient.SetEndpoints(cfg.Endpoints...)\n   491→\n   492→\t// Use a provided endpoint target so that for https:// without any tls config given, then\n   493→\t// grpc will assume the certificate server name is the endpoint host.\n   494→\tconn, err := client.dialWithBalancer()\n   495→\tif err != nil {\n   496→\t\tclient.cancel()\n   497→\t\tclient.resolver.Close()\n   498→\t\t// TODO: Error like `fmt.Errorf(dialing [%s] failed: %v, strings.Join(cfg.Endpoints, \";\"), err)` would help with debugging a lot.\n   499→\t\treturn nil, err\n   500→\t}\n   501→\tclient.conn = conn\n   502→\n   503→\tclient.Cluster = NewCluster(client)\n   504→\tclient.KV = NewKV(client)\n   505→\tclient.Lease = NewLease(client)\n   506→\tclient.Watcher = NewWatcher(client)\n   507→\tclient.Auth = NewAuth(client)\n   508→\tclient.Maintenance = NewMaintenance(client)\n   509→\n   510→\t// get token with established connection\n   511→\tctx, cancel = client.ctx, func() {}\n   512→\tif client.cfg.DialTimeout > 0 {\n   513→\t\tctx, cancel = context.WithTimeout(ctx, client.cfg.DialTimeout)\n   514→\t}\n   515→\terr = client.getToken(ctx)\n   516→\tif err != nil {\n   517→\t\tclient.Close()\n   518→\t\tcancel()\n   519→\t\t// TODO: Consider fmt.Errorf(\"communicating with [%s] failed: %v\", strings.Join(cfg.Endpoints, \";\"), err)\n   520→\t\treturn nil, err\n   521→\t}\n   522→\tcancel()\n   523→\n   524→\tif cfg.RejectOldCluster {\n   525→\t\tif err := client.checkVersion(); err != nil {\n   526→\t\t\tclient.Close()\n   527→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   528→\t\t}\n   529→\t}\n   530→\n   531→\tgo client.autoSync()\n   532→\treturn client, nil\n   533→}\n   534→\n   535→// roundRobinQuorumBackoff retries against quorum between each backoff.\n   536→// This is intended for use with a round robin load balancer.\n   537→func (c *Client) roundRobinQuorumBackoff(waitBetween time.Duration, jitterFraction float64) backoffFunc {\n   538→\treturn func(attempt uint) time.Duration {\n   539→\t\t// after each round robin across quorum, backoff for our wait between duration\n   540→\t\tn := uint(len(c.Endpoints()))\n   541→\t\tquorum := (n/2 + 1)\n   542→\t\tif attempt%quorum == 0 {\n   543→\t\t\tc.GetLogger().Debug(\"backoff\", zap.Uint(\"attempt\", attempt), zap.Uint(\"quorum\", quorum), zap.Duration(\"waitBetween\", waitBetween), zap.Float64(\"jitterFraction\", jitterFraction))\n   544→\t\t\treturn jitterUp(waitBetween, jitterFraction)\n   545→\t\t}\n   546→\t\tc.GetLogger().Debug(\"backoff skipped\", zap.Uint(\"attempt\", attempt), zap.Uint(\"quorum\", quorum))\n   547→\t\treturn 0\n   548→\t}\n   549→}\n   550→\n   551→// minSupportedVersion returns the minimum version supported, which is the previous minor release.\n   552→func minSupportedVersion() *semver.Version {\n   553→\tver := semver.Must(semver.NewVersion(version.Version))\n   554→\t// consider only major and minor version\n   555→\tver = &semver.Version{Major: ver.Major, Minor: ver.Minor}\n   556→\tfor i := range version.AllVersions {\n   557→\t\tif version.AllVersions[i].Equal(*ver) {\n   558→\t\t\tif i == 0 {\n   559→\t\t\t\treturn ver\n   560→\t\t\t}\n   561→\t\t\treturn &version.AllVersions[i-1]\n   562→\t\t}\n   563→\t}\n   564→\tpanic(\"current version is not in the version list\")\n   565→}\n   566→\n   567→func (c *Client) checkVersion() (err error) {\n   568→\tvar wg sync.WaitGroup\n   569→\n   570→\teps := c.Endpoints()\n   571→\terrc := make(chan error, len(eps))\n   572→\tctx, cancel := context.WithCancel(c.ctx)\n   573→\tif c.cfg.DialTimeout > 0 {\n   574→\t\tcancel()\n   575→\t\tctx, cancel = context.WithTimeout(c.ctx, c.cfg.DialTimeout)\n   576→\t}\n   577→\n   578→\twg.Add(len(eps))\n   579→\tfor _, ep := range eps {\n   580→\t\t// if cluster is current, any endpoint gives a recent version\n   581→\t\tgo func(e string) {\n   582→\t\t\tdefer wg.Done()\n   583→\t\t\tresp, rerr := c.Status(ctx, e)\n   584→\t\t\tif rerr != nil {\n   585→\t\t\t\terrc <- rerr\n   586→\t\t\t\treturn\n   587→\t\t\t}\n   588→\t\t\tvs, serr := semver.NewVersion(resp.Version)\n   589→\t\t\tif serr != nil {\n   590→\t\t\t\terrc <- serr\n   591→\t\t\t\treturn\n   592→\t\t\t}\n   593→\n   594→\t\t\tif vs.LessThan(*minSupportedVersion()) {\n   595→\t\t\t\trerr = ErrOldCluster\n   596→\t\t\t}\n   597→\t\t\terrc <- rerr\n   598→\t\t}(ep)\n   599→\t}\n   600→\t// wait for success\n   601→\tfor range eps {\n   602→\t\tif err = <-errc; err != nil {\n   603→\t\t\tbreak\n   604→\t\t}\n   605→\t}\n   606→\tcancel()\n   607→\twg.Wait()\n   608→\treturn err\n   609→}\n   610→\n   611→// ActiveConnection returns the current in-use connection\n   612→func (c *Client) ActiveConnection() *grpc.ClientConn { return c.conn }\n   613→\n   614→// isHaltErr returns true if the given error and context indicate no forward\n   615→// progress can be made, even after reconnecting.\n   616→func isHaltErr(ctx context.Context, err error) bool {\n   617→\tif ctx != nil && ctx.Err() != nil {\n   618→\t\treturn true\n   619→\t}\n   620→\tif err == nil {\n   621→\t\treturn false\n   622→\t}\n   623→\tev, _ := status.FromError(err)\n   624→\t// Unavailable codes mean the system will be right back.\n   625→\t// (e.g., can't connect, lost leader)\n   626→\t// Treat Internal codes as if something failed, leaving the\n   627→\t// system in an inconsistent state, but retrying could make progress.\n   628→\t// (e.g., failed in middle of send, corrupted frame)\n   629→\t// TODO: are permanent Internal errors possible from grpc?\n   630→\treturn ev.Code() != codes.Unavailable && ev.Code() != codes.Internal\n   631→}\n   632→\n   633→// isUnavailableErr returns true if the given error is an unavailable error\n   634→func isUnavailableErr(ctx context.Context, err error) bool {\n   635→\tif ctx != nil && ctx.Err() != nil {\n   636→\t\treturn false\n   637→\t}\n   638→\tif err == nil {\n   639→\t\treturn false\n   640→\t}\n   641→\tev, ok := status.FromError(err)\n   642→\tif ok {\n   643→\t\t// Unavailable codes mean the system will be right back.\n   644→\t\t// (e.g., can't connect, lost leader)\n   645→\t\treturn ev.Code() == codes.Unavailable\n   646→\t}\n   647→\treturn false\n   648→}\n   649→\n   650→// ContextError converts the error into an EtcdError if the error message matches one of\n   651→// the defined messages; otherwise, it tries to retrieve the context error.\n   652→func ContextError(ctx context.Context, err error) error {\n   653→\tif err == nil {\n   654→\t\treturn nil\n   655→\t}\n   656→\terr = rpctypes.Error(err)\n   657→\tvar serverErr rpctypes.EtcdError\n   658→\tif errors.As(err, &serverErr) {\n   659→\t\treturn err\n   660→\t}\n   661→\tif ev, ok := status.FromError(err); ok {\n   662→\t\tcode := ev.Code()\n   663→\t\tswitch code {\n   664→\t\tcase codes.DeadlineExceeded:\n   665→\t\t\tfallthrough\n   666→\t\tcase codes.Canceled:\n   667→\t\t\tif ctx.Err() != nil {\n   668→\t\t\t\terr = ctx.Err()\n   669→\t\t\t}\n   670→\t\t}\n   671→\t}\n   672→\treturn err\n   673→}\n   674→\n   675→func canceledByCaller(stopCtx context.Context, err error) bool {\n   676→\tif stopCtx.Err() == nil || err == nil {\n   677→\t\treturn false\n   678→\t}\n   679→\n   680→\treturn errors.Is(err, context.Canceled) || errors.Is(err, context.DeadlineExceeded)\n   681→}\n   682→\n   683→// IsConnCanceled returns true, if error is from a closed gRPC connection.\n   684→// ref. https://github.com/grpc/grpc-go/pull/1854\n   685→func IsConnCanceled(err error) bool {\n   686→\tif err == nil {\n   687→\t\treturn false\n   688→\t}\n   689→\n   690→\t// >= gRPC v1.23.x\n   691→\ts, ok := status.FromError(err)\n   692→\tif ok {\n   693→\t\t// connection is canceled or server has already closed the connection\n   694→\t\treturn s.Code() == codes.Canceled || s.Message() == \"transport is closing\"\n   695→\t}\n   696→\n   697→\t// >= gRPC v1.10.x\n   698→\tif errors.Is(err, context.Canceled) {\n   699→\t\treturn true\n   700→\t}\n   701→\n   702→\t// <= gRPC v1.7.x returns 'errors.New(\"grpc: the client connection is closing\")'\n   703→\treturn strings.Contains(err.Error(), \"grpc: the client connection is closing\")\n   704→}\n The health check\n\t// may return Unimplemented if the server does not expose the health endpoint,\n\t// or FailedPrecondition if the leader has not yet applied the configuration\n\t// change that enables it. In both cases, we can still treat the connection as\n\t// healthy enough to proceed.\n\t//\n\t// Use withMax to disable retrying on Unimplemented, so that we can\n\t// return the original error serr, ok := status.FromError(err); ok && serr.Message() != \"\" {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"etcdclient: failed to connect to the etcd server: %s: %w\", serr.Message(), cerr)\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn codes.FailedPrecondition:\n\t\t\treturn nil\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"etcdclient: failed to dial by invoking health endpoint: %w\", err)\n}\n\nfunc authority(endpoint string) string {\n\tspl \"unixs:\") {\n\t\t\treturn endpoint[len(\"unixs:\"):]\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn endpoint\n\t}\n\treturn spl[1]\n}\n\nfunc (c *Client) credentialsForEndpoint(ep string) grpccredentials.TransportCredentials {\n\tr := endpoint.RequiresCredentials(ep)\n\tswitch r {\n\tcase endpoint.CredsDrop:\n\t\treturn nil\n\tcase endpoint.CredsOptional:\n\t\treturn c.creds\n\tcase endpoint.CredsRequire:\n\t\tif c.creds client, nil\n}\n\n// roundRobinQuorumBackoff retries against quorum between each backoff.\n// This is intended for use with a round robin load balancer.\nfunc (c *Client) roundRobinQuorumBackoff(waitBetween time.Duration, jitterFraction float64) backoffFunc {\n\treturn func(attempt uint) time.Duration {\n\t\t// after each round robin across quorum, backoff for our wait between duration\n\t\tn := uint(len(c.Endpoints()))\n\t\tquorum := (n/2 + 1)\n\t\tif attempt%quorum == 0 {\n\t\t\tc.GetLogger().Debug(\"backoff\", zap.Uint(\"attempt\", attempt), zap.Uint(\"quorum\", quorum), zap.Duration(\"waitBetween\", waitBetween), zap.Float64(\"jitterFraction\", jitterFraction))\n\t\t\treturn jitterUp(waitBetween, jitterFraction)\n\t\t}\n\t\tc.GetLogger().Debug(\"backoff skipped\", zap.Uint(\"attempt\", attempt), zap.Uint(\"quorum\", quorum))\n\t\treturn 0\n\t}\n}\n\n// minSupportedVersion returns the minimum version supported, which is the previous minor release.\nfunc minSupportedVersion() *semver.Version {\n\tver := semver.Must(semver.NewVersion(version.Version))\n\t// consider only major and minor version\n\tver = &semver.Version{Major: ver.Major, 311→\n   312→func waitRetryBackoff(ctx context.Context, attempt uint, callOpts *options) error {\n   313→\twaitTime := time.Duration(0)\n   314→\tif attempt > 0 {\n   315→\t\twaitTime = 349→\t\treturn isSafeRetryMutableRPC(err)\n   350→\tdefault:\n   351→\t\tc.GetLogger().Warn(\"unrecognized retry policy\", zap.String(\"retryPolicy\", callOpts.retryPolicy.String()))\n   352→\t\treturn false\n   353→\t}\n   354→}\n   355→\n   356→func isContextError(err error) bool {\n   357→\treturn status.Code(err) == codes.DeadlineExceeded || status.Code(err) == codes.Canceled\n err.Error())\n   368→\t}\n   369→}\n   370→\n   371→var defaultOptions = &options{\n   372→\tretryPolicy: nonRepeatable,\n   373→\tmax:         0, // disable\n   374→\tbackoffFunc: backoffLinearWithJitter(50*time.Millisecond /*jitter*/, 0.10),\n   375→\tretryAuth:   true,\n   376→}\n   377→\n   378→// backoffFunc denotes a family of functions that control the backoff duration between call retries.\n   379→//\n   380→// They are called with an identifier of the attempt, and should return a time the system client should\n   381→// hold off for. This behaviour can be\n// changed through options (e.g. WithMax) on creation of the interceptor or on call (through grpc.CallOptions).\nfunc (c *Client) unaryClientInterceptor(optFuncs ...retryOption) grpc.UnaryClientInterceptor {\n\tintOpts := reuseOrNewWithCallOptions(defaultOptions, optFuncs)\n\treturn func(ctx context.Context, method string, req, reply any, cc *grpc.ClientConn, invoker grpc.UnaryInvoker, opts ...grpc.CallOption) error {\n\t\tctx = withVersion(ctx)\n\t\tgrpcOpts, retryOpts := filterCallOptions(opts)\n\t\tvar p peer.Peer\n\t\tgrpcOpts = append(grpcOpts, grpc.Peer(&p))\n\t\tcallOpts := reuseOrNewWithCallOptions(intOpts, retryOpts)\n\t\t// short circuit for simplicity, and avoiding allocations.\n\t\tif callOpts.max == 0 {\n\t\t\treturn invoker(ctx, method, req, reply, cc, grpcOpts...)\n\t\t}\n\t\tvar lastErr error\n\t\tfor attempt := uint(0); attempt < callOpts.max; attempt++ {\n\t\t\tif err := waitRetryBackoff(ctx, attempt, callOpts); err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tc.GetLogger().Debug(\n\t\t\t\t\"retrying of unary invoker\",\n\t\t\t\tzap.String(\"target\", cc.Target()),\n\t\t\t\tzap.String(\"method\", method),\n\t\t\t\tzap.Uint(\"attempt\", attempt),\n\t\t\t)\n\t\t\tlastErr = invoker(ctx, method, req, reply, cc, grpcOpts...)\n\t\t\tif lastErr == nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tc.GetLogger().Warn(\n\t\t\t\t\"retrying of unary invoker failed\",\n\t\t\t\tzap.String(\"target\", cc.Target()),\n\t\t\t\tzap.String(\"peer\", p.String()),\n\t\t\t\tzap.String(\"method\", method),\n\t\t\t\tzap.Uint(\"attempt\", attempt),\n\t\t\t\tzap.Error(lastErr),\n\t\t\t)\n\t\t\tif isContextError(lastErr) {\n\t\t\t\tif ctx.Err() != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\t// its the context deadline or cancellation.\n\t\t\t\t\treturn lastErr\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t// its the callCtx deadline or cancellation, in which case try again.\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif c.shouldRefreshToken(lastErr, callOpts) {\n\t\t\t\tgtErr := c.refreshToken(ctx)\n\t\t\t\tif gtErr != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\tc.GetLogger().Warn(\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\"retrying of unary invoker failed to fetch new auth token\",\n\t\t\t\t\t\tzap.String(\"target\", cc.Target()),\n\t\t\t\t\t\tzap.Error(gtErr),\n\t\t\t\t\t)\n\t\t\t\t\treturn gtErr // lastErr must be invalid auth token\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif !isSafeRetry(c, lastErr, callOpts) {\n\t\t\t\treturn lastErr\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn lastErr\n\t}\n}\n\n// streamClientInterceptor returns a new retrying stream client interceptor for server side streaming calls.\n//\n// The default configuration of the interceptor is to not retry *at all*. This behaviour can be\n// changed through options (e.g. WithMax) on creation of the interceptor or on call (through grpc.CallOptions).\n//\n// Retry logic is available *only for ServerStreams*, i.e. 1:n streams, as the internal logic needs\n// to buffer the messages sent by the client. If retry is enabled on any other streams (ClientStreams,\n// BidiStreams), the retry interceptor will fail the call.\nfunc (c *Client) streamClientInterceptor(optFuncs ...retryOption) grpc.StreamClientInterceptor {\n\tintOpts := reuseOrNewWithCallOptions(defaultOptions, optFuncs)\n\treturn func(ctx context.Context, desc *grpc.StreamDesc, cc *grpc.ClientConn, method string, streamer grpc.Streamer, opts ...grpc.CallOption) (grpc.ClientStream, error) {\n\t\tctx = withVersion(ctx)\n\t\t// getToken automatically. Otherwise, auth token may be invalid after watch reconnection because the token has expired\n\t\t// (see https://github.com/etcd-io/etcd/issues/11954 for more).\n\t\terr := c.getToken(ctx)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tc.GetLogger().Error(\"clientv3/retry_interceptor: getToken failed\", zap.Error(err))\n\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t}\n\t\tgrpcOpts, retryOpts := filterCallOptions(opts)\n\t\tcallOpts := reuseOrNewWithCallOptions(intOpts, retryOpts)\n\t\t// short circuit for simplicity, and avoiding allocations.\n\t\tif callOpts.max == 0 {\n\t\t\treturn streamer(ctx, desc, cc, method, grpcOpts...)\n\t\t}\n\t\tif desc.ClientStreams {\n\t\t\treturn nil, status.Errorf(codes.Unimplemented, \"clientv3/retry_interceptor: cannot retry on ClientStreams, set Disable()\")\n\t\t}\n\t\tnewStreamer, err := streamer(ctx, desc, cc, method, grpcOpts...)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tc.GetLogger().Error(\"streamer failed to create ClientStream\", zap.Error(err))\n\t\t\treturn nil, err // TODO(mwitkow): Maybe dial and transport errors should be retriable?\n\t\t}\n\t\tretryingStreamer := &serverStreamingRetryingStream{\n\t\t\tclient: desc, cc, method, grpcOpts...)\n\t\t\t},\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn retryingStreamer, nil\n\t}\n}\n\n// shouldRefreshToken checks whether there's a need to refresh the token based on the error and callOptions,\n// and returns a boolean value.\nfunc (c *Client) shouldRefreshToken(err error, callOpts *options) bool {\n\tif c.Token != \"\" {\n\t\t// do not try to refresh the token as it is set by user\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\n\tif errors.Is(rpctypes.Error(err), rpctypes.ErrUserEmpty) {\n\t\t// refresh the token when username, password is present but the server returns ErrUserEmpty\n\t\t// which is possible when the client token is cleared somehow\n\t\treturn c.authTokenBundle != nil // equal to c.Username != \"\" && c.Password != \"\"\n\t}\n\n\treturn callOpts.retryAuth &&\n\t\t(errors.Is(rpctypes.Error(err), rpctypes.ErrInvalidAuthToken) || errors.Is(rpctypes.Error(err), rpctypes.ErrAuthOldRevision))\n}\n\nfunc (c *Client) refreshToken(ctx context.Context) error {\n\tif c.authTokenBundle == nil {\n\t\t// c.authTokenBundle will be initialized only when\n\t\t// c.Username != \"\" && c.Password != \"\".\n\t\t//\n\t\t// When users use the TLS CommonName based authentication, the\n\t\t// authTokenBundle is always nil. But it's possible for the clients\n\t\t// to get `rpctypes.ErrAuthOldRevision` response when the clients\n\t\t// concurrently modify auth data (e.g, addUser, deleteUser etc.).\n\t\t// In this case, there is no need to refresh the token; instead the\n\t\t// clients just need to retry the operations (e.g. Put, Delete etc).\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\n\treturn c.getToken(ctx)\n}\n\n// type serverStreamingRetryingStream is the implementation of grpc.ClientStream that acts as a\n// proxy to the underlying call. If any of the RecvMsg() calls fail, it will try to reestablish\n// a new ClientStream according to the retry policy.\ntype serverStreamingRetryingStream struct {\n\tgrpc.ClientStream\n\tclient *serverStreamingRetryingStream) setStream(clientStream grpc.ClientStream) {\n\ts.mu.Lock()\n\ts.ClientStream = clientStream\n\ts.mu.Unlock()\n}\n\nfunc (s *serverStreamingRetryingStream) getStream() grpc.ClientStream {\n\ts.mu.RLock()\n\tdefer s.mu.RUnlock()\n\treturn s.ClientStream\n}\n\nfunc (s *serverStreamingRetryingStream) SendMsg(m any) error {\n\ts.mu.Lock()\n\ts.bufferedSends = append(s.bufferedSends, m)\n\ts.mu.Unlock()\n\treturn s.getStream().SendMsg(m)\n}\n\nfunc (s *serverStreamingRetryingStream) CloseSend() error {\n\ts.mu.Lock()\n\ts.wasClosedSend = true\n\ts.mu.Unlock()\n\treturn s.getStream().CloseSend()\n}\n\nfunc (s *serverStreamingRetryingStream) Header() (metadata.MD, error) {\n\treturn s.getStream().Header()\n}\n\nfunc (s *serverStreamingRetryingStream) Trailer() metadata.MD {\n\treturn s.getStream().Trailer()\n}\n\nfunc (s *serverStreamingRetryingStream) RecvMsg(m any) error {\n\tattemptRetry, lastErr := s.receiveMsgAndIndicateRetry(m)\n\tif !attemptRetry {\n\t\treturn lastErr // success or hard failure\n\t}\n\n\t// We start off from attempt 1, because zeroth was already made on normal SendMsg().\n\tfor attempt := uint(1); attempt < s.callOpts.max; attempt++ {\n\t\tif err := waitRetryBackoff(s.ctx, attempt, s.callOpts); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t}\n\t\tnewStream, err := s.reestablishStreamAndResendBuffer(s.ctx)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\ts.client.GetLogger().Error(\"failed reestablishStreamAndResendBuffer\", zap.Error(err))\n\t\t\treturn err // TODO(mwitkow): Maybe dial and transport errors should be retriable?\n\t\t}\n\t\ts.setStream(newStream)\n\n\t\ts.client.GetLogger().Warn(\"retrying RecvMsg\", zap.Error(lastErr))\n\t\tattemptRetry, lastErr = s.receiveMsgAndIndicateRetry(m)\n\t\tif !attemptRetry {\n\t\t\treturn lastErr\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn lastErr\n}\n\nfunc (s *serverStreamingRetryingStream) receiveMsgAndIndicateRetry(m any) (bool, error) {\n\ts.mu.RLock()\n\twasGood := s.receivedGood\n\ts.mu.RUnlock()\n\terr := s.getStream().RecvMsg(m)\n\tif err == nil || errors.Is(err, io.EOF) {\n\t\ts.mu.Lock()\n\t\ts.receivedGood = true\n\t\ts.mu.Unlock()\n\t\treturn false, err\n\t} else if wasGood {\n\t\t// previous RecvMsg in the stream succeeded, no retry logic should interfere\n\t\treturn false, err\n\t}\n\tif isContextError(err) {\n\t\tif s.ctx.Err() != nil {\n\t\t\treturn false, err\n\t\t}\n\t\t// its the callCtx deadline or cancellation, in which case try again.\n\t\treturn true, err\n\t}\n\tif s.client.shouldRefreshToken(err, s.callOpts) {\n\t\tgtErr := s.client.refreshToken(s.ctx)\n\t\tif gtErr != nil {\n\t\t\ts.client.GetLogger().Warn(\"retry failed to fetch new auth token\", zap.Error(gtErr))\n\t\t\treturn false, err // return the original error for simplicity\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn true, err\n\t}\n\treturn isSafeRetry(s.client, err, s.callOpts), err\n}\n\nfunc (s *serverStreamingRetryingStream) reestablishStreamAndResendBuffer(callCtx context.Context) (grpc.ClientStream, error) {\n\ts.mu.RLock()\n\tbufferedSends := s.bufferedSends\n\ts.mu.RUnlock()\n\tnewStream, err := s.streamerCall(callCtx)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\tfor _, msg := range bufferedSends {\n\t\tif err := newStream.SendMsg(msg); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tif err := newStream.CloseSend(); err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\treturn newStream, nil\n}\n\nfunc waitRetryBackoff(ctx context.Context, attempt uint, callOpts *options) error {\n\twaitTime := time.Duration(0)\n\tif attempt > 0 {\n\t\twaitTime = callOpts.backoffFunc(attempt)\n\t}\n\tif waitTime > 0 {\n\t\ttimer := time.NewTimer(waitTime)\n\t\tselect {\n\t\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n\t\t\ttimer.Stop()\n\t\t\treturn contextErrToGRPCErr(ctx.Err())\n\t\tcase <-timer.C:\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// isSafeRetry returns \"true\", if request is safe for retry with the given error.\nfunc isSafeRetry(c *Client, err error, callOpts *options) bool {\n\tif isContextError(err) {\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\n\t// Situation when learner refuses RPC it is supposed to not serve is from the server\n\t// perspective not retryable.\n\t// But for backward-compatibility reasons we need  to support situation that\n\t// customer provides mix of learners (not yet voters) and voters with an\n\t// expectation to pick voter in the next attempt.\n\t// TODO: Ideally client should be 'aware' which endpoint represents: leader/voter/learner with high probability.\n\tif errors.Is(err, rpctypes.ErrGRPCNotSupportedForLearner) && len(c.Endpoints()) > 1 {\n\t\treturn true\n\t}\n\n\tswitch callOpts.retryPolicy {\n\tcase repeatable:\n\t\treturn isSafeRetryImmutableRPC(err)\n\tcase nonRepeatable:\n\t\treturn isSafeRetryMutableRPC(err)\n\tdefault:\n\t\tc.GetLogger().Warn(\"unrecognized retry policy\", zap.String(\"retryPolicy\", callOpts.retryPolicy.String()))\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc isContextError(err error) bool {\n\treturn status.Code(err) == codes.DeadlineExceeded || status.Code(err) == codes.Canceled\n}\n\nfunc contextErrToGRPCErr(err error) error {\n\tswitch {\n\tcase errors.Is(err, context.DeadlineExceeded):\n\t\treturn status.Error(codes.DeadlineExceeded, err.Error())\n\tcase errors.Is(err, context.Canceled):\n\t\treturn status.Error(codes.Canceled, err.Error())\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn status.Error(codes.Unknown, err.Error())\n\t}\n}\n\nvar defaultOptions = &options{\n\tretryPolicy: nonRepeatable,\n\tmax:         0, // disable\n\tbackoffFunc: backoffLinearWithJitter(50*time.Millisecond /*jitter*/, 0.10),\n\tretryAuth:   true,\n}\n\n// backoffFunc denotes a family of functions that control the backoff duration between call retries.\n//\n// They are called with an identifier of the attempt, and should return a time the system client should\n// hold off for. error\n\t\t// client cannot handle itself (e.g. rpctypes.ErrCompacted)\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\t// only retry if unavailable\n\tev, ok := status.FromError(err)\n\tif !ok {\n\t\t// all errors from RPC is typed \"grpc/status.(*statusError)\"\n\t\t// (ref. https://github.com/grpc/grpc-go/pull/1782)\n\t\t//\n\t\t// if the error type is not \"grpc/status.(*statusError)\",\n\t\t// it could be from \"Dial\"\n\t\t// TODO: do not retry for now\n\t\t// ref. https://github.com/grpc/grpc-go/issues/1581\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\treturn ev.Code() == codes.Unavailable\n}\n\n// isSafeRetryMutableRPC returns \"true\" when a mutable request is safe for retry.\n//\n// mutable requests (e.g. Put, Delete, Txn) should only be retried\n// when the status code is codes.Unavailable when initial connection\n// has not been established (no endpoint is up).\n//\n// Returning \"false\" means retry should stop, otherwise it violates\n// write-at-most-once semantics.\nfunc isSafeRetryMutableRPC(err error) bool {\n\tif ev, ok := status.FromError(err); ok && ev.Code() != codes.Unavailable {\n\t\t// not safe for mutable RPCs\n\t\t// e.g. interrupted by non-transient error that client cannot handle itself,\n\t\t// or transient error while the connection has already been established\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\tdesc := rpctypes.ErrorDesc(err)\n\treturn desc == \"there is no address available\" || desc == \"there is no connection available\"\n}\n\ntype retryKVClient struct {\n\tkc pb.KVClient\n}\n\n// RetryKVClient implements a KVClient.\nfunc RetryKVClient(c *Client) passed WithRev(rev) with rev > 0, Get retrieves keys at the given revision;\n\t// if the required revision is compacted, the request will fail with ErrCompacted .\n\t// When passed WithLimit(limit), arbitrary operations to be issued at a\n\t// later time; the user can range over the operations, calling Do to\n\t// execute them. Get/Put/Delete, on the other hand, are best suited\n\t// for when the operation should be issued at the time of declaration.\n\tDo(ctx context.Context, op Op) (OpResponse, error)\n\n\t// Txn creates a string) {\n\tspl := strings.SplitN(s, sep, 2)\n\tif len(spl) < 2 {\n\t\tpanic(fmt.Errorf(\"token '%v' expected to have separator sep: `%v`\", s, sep))\n\t}\n\treturn spl[0], spl[1]\n}\n\nfunc schemeToCredsRequirement(schema string) CredsRequirement {\n\tswitch schema {\n\tcase \"https\", \"unixs\":\n\t\treturn CredsRequire\n\tcase \"http\":\n\t\treturn CredsDrop\n\tcase \"unix\":\n\t\t// Preserving previous behavior from:\n\t\t// https://github.com/etcd-io/etcd/blob/dae29bb719dd69dc119146fc297a0628fcc1ccf8/client/v3/client.go#L212\n\t\t// that likely was a bug due to missing CredsOptional\n\tcase \"\":\n\t\treturn CredsOptional\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn CredsOptional\n\t}\n}\n\n// This function translates endpoints names supported by etcd server into\n// endpoints as supported by grpc with additional information\n// (server_name for cert validation, requireCreds - whether certs are needed).\n// The main differences:\n//   - etcd supports unixs & https names as opposed to unix & http to\n//     distinguish need to configure certificates.\n//   - etcd support http(s) names as opposed to tcp supported by grpc/dial method.\n//   - etcd supports unix(s)://local-file naming schema\n//     (as opposed to unix:local-file canonical name used by grpc for current dir files).\n//   - Within the unix(s) schemas, the last segment (filename) without 'port' (content after colon)\n//     is considered serverName - to allow local testing of cert-protected communication.\n//\n// See more:\n//   - https://github.com/grpc/grpc-go/blob/26c143bd5f59344a4b8a1e491e0f5e18aa97abc7/internal/grpcutil/target.go#L47\n//   - https://golang.org/pkg/net/#Dial\n//   - https://github.com/grpc/grpc/blob/master/doc/naming.md\nfunc translateEndpoint(ep string) (addr string, serverName string, requireCreds CredsRequirement) {\n\tif strings.HasPrefix(ep, \"unix:\") || strings.HasPrefix(ep, \"unixs:\") {\n\t\tif strings.HasPrefix(ep, \"unix:///\") || strings.HasPrefix(ep, \"unixs:///\") {\n\t\t\t// absolute path case\n\t\t\tschema, absolutePath := mustSplit2(ep, \"://\")\n\t\t\treturn \"unix://\" + absolutePath, path.Base(absolutePath), schemeToCredsRequirement(schema)\n\t\t}\n\t\tif strings.HasPrefix(ep, \"unix://\") || strings.HasPrefix(ep, \"unixs://\") localPath := mustSplit2(ep, \":\")\n\t\treturn \"unix:\" + localPath, path.Base(localPath), schemeToCredsRequirement(schema)\n\t}\n\n\tif strings.Contains(ep, \"://\") {\n\t\turl, err := url.Parse(ep)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn ep, ep, CredsOptional\n\t\t}\n\t\tif url.Scheme == \"http\" || url.Scheme == \"https\" {\n\t\t\treturn url.Host, url.Host, schemeToCredsRequirement(url.Scheme)\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn ep, url.Host, schemeToCredsRequirement(url.Scheme)\n\t}\n\t// Handles plain addresses like 10.0.0.44:437.\n\treturn ep, ep, CredsOptional\n}\n\n// RequiresCredentials returns whether given endpoint requires\n// credentials/certificates for connection.\nfunc RequiresCredentials(ep string) CredsRequirement {\n\t_, _, address (supported by 'net') to connect to,\n// and a server name used for x509 certificate matching.\nfunc Interpret(ep string) (address string, serverName string) {\n\taddr, serverName, _ := and can reestablish streams\\n- **isSafeRetry**: Determines whether a request can be safely retried based on the error type and retry policy (repeatable vs. nonRepeatable)\\n- **waitRetryBackoff**: 263-272), where:\\n- Unary RPCs get up to 100 retries by default (configurable via MaxUnaryRetries in Config)\\n- Stream RPCs are disabled by default (withMax(0)) except for specific operations like Endpoint Balancer\\n\\nThe endpoint balancer is implemented using gRPC's resolver pattern:\\n- **EtcdManualResolver** in `client/v3/internal/resolver/resolver.go`: A manual resolver that implements round-robin load balancing (line 44: `\\\"loadBalancingPolicy\\\": \\\"round_robin\\\"`)\\n- The resolver is initialized in `client/v3/client.go:newClient` (line 484) and used in `dialWithBalancer` (line 314)\\n- **Endpoint translation** in `client/v3/internal/endpoint/endpoint.go`: Handles parsing of various endpoint formats (http, https, unix, unixs) and determines whether credentials are required\\n- **Endpoint management** in `client/v3/naming/endpoints/`: Provides Manager interface and endpointManager implementation for managing service endpoints stored in etcd\\n\\n## 3. Connection Health Check\\n\\nConnection health verification is implemented in `client/v3/client.go:waitForConnection` (lines 345-375):\\n- Uses gRPC health check protocol (HealthCheckRequest via google.golang.org/grpc/health)\\n- Called during connection establishment to verify the connection is ready\\n- Gracefully handles Unimplemented and FailedPrecondition errors for servers without health endpoint\\n- Integrated into the dial process with configurable DialTimeout\\n\\n## 4. Request Timeout Enforcement\\n\\nTimeout enforcement is distributed across operation types:\\n\\n### KV Operations (client/v3/kv.go)\\n- KV interface defines Put, Get, Delete, Compact, and Txn operations\\n- All KV methods accept context with potential timeout: `Put(ctx context.Context, key, val string, opts ...OpOption)`\\n- Uses RetryKVClient wrapper from retry.go that applies repeatable policy to Range operations and default policy to write operations\\n- Timeout is enforced through context cancellation passed through the gRPC interceptors\\n\\n### Watch Operations (client/v3/watch.go)\\n- Watcher interface with Watch method accepting context: `Watch(ctx context.Context, key string, opts ...OpOption) WatchChan`\\n- watchGRPCStream manages the watch stream lifecycle with reconnection logic (lines 156-188)\\n- Watch operations use a reduced backoff strategy (closeSendErrTimeout = 250ms at line 37)\\n- Stream retries are disabled by default (withMax(0)) but the stream layer handles reconnection internally\\n\\n### Lease Operations (client/v3/lease.go)\\n- Lease interface defines Grant, Revoke, TimeToLive, Leases, KeepAlive, and KeepAliveOnce operations\\n- KeepAlive uses a separate stream with custom timeout handling via firstKeepAliveTimeout (default: DialTimeout + 1 second, lines 192-194)\\n- keepAlive multiplexer tracks deadline for each lease (line 184: `deadline: time.Now().Add(l.firstKeepAliveTimeout)`)\\n- LeaseKeepAlive stream retry is disabled via `withMax(0)` but the stream is internally managed and reconnected\\n\\n## 5. Configuration and Defaults\\n\\nTimeout and retry configuration is defined in:\\n- **Config structure** (client/v3/config.go): DialTimeout, DialKeepAliveTime, DialKeepAliveTimeout, MaxUnaryRetries, BackoffWaitBetween, BackoffJitterFraction\\n- **Default values** (client/v3/options.go):\\n  - defaultUnaryMaxRetries: 100\\n  - defaultBackoffWaitBetween: 25ms\\n  - defaultBackoffJitterFraction: 0.10\\n  - defaultWaitForReady: true (enables client-side retrying for transient failures)\\n\\n## 6. Retry Policies\\n\\nRetry safety determination in `client/v3/retry.go`:\\n- **isSafeRetryImmutableRPC**: Allows retries for immutable operations (Get, Range) on codes.Unavailable\\n- **isSafeRetryMutableRPC**: Restricts retries for mutable operations (Put, Delete) only on Unavailable with no address available\\n- Policy application through RetryKVClient, RetryLeaseClient, RetryClusterClient, RetryMaintenanceClient, and RetryAuthClient wrappers\\n\\nThe retry and timeout mechanisms work together through the interceptor chain to provide reliable client operations with appropriate backoff and deadline enforcement across KV, Watch, and Lease operations.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":5,"cache_creation_input_tokens":832,"cache_read_input_tokens":79816,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":832},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"480b5654-61a3-4314-abdd-da1330c5d834","uuid":"8b50d913-eaba-4cef-bf57-7b537723ac33"}

Request Timeout Enforcement\\n\\nTimeout enforcement is distributed across operation types:\\n\\n### KV Operations (client/v3/kv.go)\\n- KV interface defines Put, Get, Delete, Compact, and Txn operations\\n- All KV methods accept context with potential timeout: `Put(ctx context.Context, key, val string, opts ...OpOption)`\\n- Uses RetryKVClient wrapper from retry.go that applies repeatable policy to Range operations and default policy to write operations\\n- Timeout is enforced through context cancellation passed through the gRPC interceptors\\n\\n### Watch Operations (client/v3/watch.go)\\n- Watcher interface with Watch method accepting context: `Watch(ctx context.Context, key string, opts ...OpOption) WatchChan`\\n- watchGRPCStream manages the watch stream lifecycle with reconnection logic (lines 156-188)\\n- Watch operations use a reduced backoff strategy (closeSendErrTimeout = 250ms at line 37)\\n- Stream retries are disabled by default (withMax(0)) but the stream layer handles reconnection internally\\n\\n### Lease Operations (client/v3/lease.go)\\n- Lease interface defines Grant, Revoke, TimeToLive, Leases, KeepAlive, and KeepAliveOnce operations\\n- KeepAlive uses a separate stream with custom timeout handling via firstKeepAliveTimeout (default: DialTimeout + 1 second, lines 192-194)\\n- keepAlive multiplexer tracks deadline for each lease (line 184: `deadline: time.Now().Add(l.firstKeepAliveTimeout)`)\\n- LeaseKeepAlive stream retry is disabled via `withMax(0)` but the stream is internally managed and reconnected\\n\\n## 5.
